      var el = document.querySelector('style[data-hide-bottom-popup]'); 
      if(el) {
        el.remove();
        document.removeEventListener('click', handleClickHidePopup);

    const lastScrollY = window.scrollY;
    window.addEventListener('scroll', function handleScrollHidePopup() {
      if(Math.abs(window.scrollY - lastScrollY) > 16){
        var el = document.querySelector('style[data-hide-bottom-popup]'); 
        if(el) {
          el.remove();
          window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScrollHidePopup);
        }
      }
    });
